////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
// 365 day DHW Profile by number of Bedrooms
//
// There are 65 profiles:
//  - 5 single family profiles. One for each house size 1-5 bedrooms
//    (DHW1BR-DHW5BR)
//  - 60 multifamily profiles. 10 sets of 6 for each dwelling unit size studio-5
//    bedrooms (DHW0BR-DHW5BR). Each set is a different shuffling of the annual
//    profile to introduce diversity of draws amond units in the same building.
//    Each multifamily shuffling is designated a different letter suffix (a-j).
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
// Each day is given a code: <Occupancy Level><Day Type><Profile Number>
//
// Occupancy levels are 1-6, representing the number of people residing in the
//  house that the draw comes from (6 = 6 or more people).
//
// Day type is one of:
//  - D (Weekday)
//  - E (Weekend)
//  - H (Holiday)
//
// Profile number: For each combination of occupancy level and day type, there
//  are several representative day profiles selected (see Kruis report for
//  methodology). The profiles are selected from equal spaced bins of all
//  days in the measurement data set based on daily total water use. There are
//  10 bins for weekdays and weekends, and 4 bins for holidays (due to sample
//  size limitations).
//
//  For example, weekdays have profile numbers 0-9. 0 being the day selected
//  from the bin with the lowest daily totals, and 9 being the day selected from
//  the bin with the highest daily totals.
//
// e.g., "4D8" is the ninth (hence 8 with index zero) weekday profile from a
//  four person home
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// #define ShwrFLOWF 1
// #define ShwrDRAINHREFF 0
// #define CwshHOTF 0.22
// #define CwshUSEF 1
// #define FaucHOTF 0.50
// #define BathFLOWF 1
// #define BathDRAINHREFF 0
// #define DwshFLOWF 1
// ============================================

// define macros for each end use (with specific parameters exposed)
#define SHWR( s, d, f, id)  \
DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="Shower" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*ShwrFLOWF wuTemp=105 wuHeatRecEF=ShwrDRAINHREFF wuEventID=id

#define CWSH( s, d, f, id) \
DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="CWashr" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*CwshUSEF wuHotF=CwshHOTF wuEventID=id

// Faucet Plan A -- deferred
// #define FaucFLOWF 1.0
// #define FaucDRAINHREFF 0
// #define FAUC( s, d, f, id) \
// DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="Faucet" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*FaucFLOWF wuTemp=70 wuHeatRecEF=FaucDRAINHREFF wuEventID=id

// Faucet Plan B
#define FAUC( s, d, f, id) \
DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="Faucet" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*FaucFLOWF wuHotF=FaucHOTF wuEventID=id

#define BATH( s, d, f, id) \
DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="Bath" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*BathFLOWF wuTemp=105 wuHeatRecEF=BathDRAINHREFF wuEventID=id

#define DWSH( s, d, f, id) \
DHWUSE wuHWEndUse="DWashr" wuStart=s wuDuration=d wuFlow=f*DwshFLOWF wuEventID=id
